Key components built:\n\n- **Binary Log (Binlog) System**: All write operations logged in LevelDB for replication\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: One master with multiple slave replicas\n- **Master-Master Replication**: Bi-directional replication between peers\n- **TCP-based Replication Protocol**: Streaming with position tracking\n- **Automatic Recovery**: Slaves reconnect and catch up on missed data\n- **Replication Commands**: `SHOW MASTER STATUS`, `CHANGE MASTER TO`, `START SLAVE`, `STOP SLAVE`, `SHOW SLAVE STATUS`\n- **Client Libraries**: PHP (`LevelDBClient.php`) and Python (`leveldb_client.py`) with replication examples\n\n### Decisions Made\n- Use **LevelDB-stored binary log** instead of MySQL-style file-based binlog\n- **Simpler than MySQL replication** - <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>distributed_tx.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nDistributed Transaction Coordinator for Multi-Node Consistency\n\nImplements Two-Phase Commit (2PC) protocol for distributed transactions.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport socket\nimport threading\nimport json\nimport time\nimport uuid\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Tuple\nfrom enum import Enum, auto\nfrom collections import defaultdict\nimport select\n\n\nclass TransactionState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"States in the 2PC protocol.\"\"\"\n    INIT = \"init\"\n    PREPARING = \"preparing\"\n    PREPARED = \"prepared\"\n    COMMITTING = \"committing\"\n    COMMITTED = \"committed\"\n    ABORTING = \"aborting\"\n    ABORTED = \"aborted\"\n    FAILED = \"failed\"\n\n\nclass ParticipantState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Participant states in 2PC.\"\"\"\n    WAITING = \"waiting\"\n    PREPARED = \"prepared\"\n    COMMITTED = \"committed\"\n    ABORTED = \"aborted\"\n    FAILED = \"failed\"\n\n\nclass DistributedTransaction:\n    \"\"\"Represents a distributed transaction.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, tx_id: str, coordinator: str, participants: List[str]):\n        self.tx_id = tx_id\n        self.coordinator = coordinator\n        self.participants = participants\n        self.state = TransactionState.INIT\n        self.participant_states: Dict[str, ParticipantState] = {\n            p: ParticipantState.WAITING for p in participants\n        }\n        self.operations: List[Dict] = []\n        self.start_time = time.time()\n        self.end_time: Optional[float] = None\n        self.result: Optional[str] = None\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n    \n    def update_state(self, new_state: TransactionState):\n        \"\"\"Update transaction state.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            self.state = new_state\n            if new_state in (TransactionState.COMMITTED, TransactionState.ABORTED, \n                           TransactionState.FAILED):\n                self.end_time = time.time()\n    \n    def update_participant(self, participant: str, state: ParticipantState):\n        \"\"\"Update participant state.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            self.participant_states[participant] = state\n    \n    def all_prepared(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if all participants are prepared.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return all(s == ParticipantState.PREPARED \n                      for s in self.participant_states.values())\n    \n    def any_aborted(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if any participant aborted.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return any(s == ParticipantState.ABORTED \n                      for s in self.participant_states.values())\n    \n    def any_failed(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Check if any participant failed.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return any(s == ParticipantState.FAILED \n                      for s in self.participant_states.values())\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Convert to dictionary.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return {\n                'tx_id': self.tx_id,\n                'coordinator': self.coordinator,\n                'state': self.state.value,\n                'participants': self.participants,\n                'participant_states': {k: v.value for k, v in self.participant_states.items()},\n                'operations': self.operations,\n                'start_time': self.start_time,\n                'end_time': self.end_time,\n                'duration': (self.end_time or time.time()) - self.start_time\n            }\n\n\nclass ParticipantConnection:\n    \"\"\"Connection to a remote participant node.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, host: str, port: int):\n        self.node_id = node_id\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.socket: Optional[socket.socket] = None\n        self.connected = False\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n    \n    def connect(self) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Connect to participant.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            self.socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n            self.socket.settimeout(10)\n            self.socket.connect((self.host, self.port))\n            self.connected = True\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[DIST-TX] Failed to connect to {self.node_id}: {e}\")\n            return False\n    \n    def disconnect(self):\n        \"\"\"Disconnect from participant.\"\"\"\n        if self.socket:\n            try:\n                self.socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n        self.socket = None\n        self.connected = False\n    \n    def send(self, message: Dict) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Send message to participant.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if not self.connected and not self.connect():\n                return False\n            \n            try:\n                data = json.dumps(message).encode()\n                self.socket.sendall(len(data).to_bytes(4, 'big') + data)\n                return True\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[DIST-TX] Send failed to {self.node_id}: {e}\")\n                self.disconnect()\n                return False\n    \n    def receive(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Receive response from participant.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if not self.connected:\n                return None\n            \n            try:\n                self.socket.settimeout(timeout)\n                \n                # Read length prefix\n                len_bytes = self.socket.recv(4)\n                if len(len_bytes) != 4:\n                    return None\n                \n                msg_len = int.from_bytes(len_bytes, 'big')\n                \n                # Read message\n                data = b''\n                while len(data) < msg_len:\n                    chunk = self.socket.recv(min(4096, msg_len - len(data)))\n                    if not chunk:\n                        return None\n                    data += chunk\n                \n                return json.loads(data.decode())\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[DIST-TX] Receive failed from {self.node_id}: {e}\")\n                self.disconnect()\n                return None\n    \n    def send_receive(self, message: Dict, timeout: float = 30.0) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Send message and receive response.\"\"\"\n        if self.send(message):\n            return self.receive(timeout)\n        return None\n\n\nclass DistributedTransactionCoordinator:\n    \"\"\"\n    Coordinator for distributed transactions using 2PC.\n    Runs on a dedicated node or as part of the database server.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, host: str = \"0.0.0.0\", port: int = 9000):\n        self.node_id = node_id\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        \n        self.participants: Dict[str, ParticipantConnection] = {}\n        self.transactions: Dict[str, DistributedTransaction] = {}\n        self.tx_log: List[Dict] = []  # Write-ahead log\n        \n        self.running = False\n        self.server_socket: Optional[socket.socket] = None\n        self._lock = threading.Lock()\n        self._recovery_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n    \n    def add_participant(self, node_id: str, host: str, port: int):\n        \"\"\"Add a participant node.\"\"\"\n        self.participants[node_id] = ParticipantConnection(node_id, host, port)\n        print(f\"[DIST-TX] Added participant {node_id} at {host}:{port}\")\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start the coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self.running = True\n        \n        # Start recovery thread\n        self._recovery_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._recovery_worker, daemon=True)\n        self._recovery_thread.start()\n        \n        # Start server\n        self.server_socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n        self.server_socket.setsockopt(socket.SOL_SOCKET, socket.SO_REUSEADDR, 1)\n        self.server_socket.bind((self.host, self.port))\n        self.server_socket.listen(10)\n        \n        print(f\"[DIST-TX] Coordinator listening on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n        \n        # Accept connections in main thread\n        while self.running:\n            try:\n                self.server_socket.settimeout(1.0)\n                client_socket, address = self.server_socket.accept()\n                handler = threading.Thread(\n                    target=self._handle_client,\n                    args=(client_socket, address),\n                    daemon=True\n                )\n                handler.start()\n            except socket.timeout:\n                continue\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[DIST-TX] Server error: {e}\")\n                break\n        \n        self.stop()\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop the coordinator.\"\"\"\n        self.running = False\n        \n        # Disconnect all participants\n        for conn in self.participants.values():\n            conn.disconnect()\n        \n        # Close server socket\n        if self.server_socket:\n            try:\n                self.server_socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n        \n        print(\"[DIST-TX] Coordinator stopped\")\n    \n    def _handle_client(self, client_socket: socket.socket, address: Tuple[str, int]):\n        \"\"\"Handle incoming client connection.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            while self.running:\n                # Read message length\n                client_socket.settimeout(1.0)\n                try:\n                    len_bytes = client_socket.recv(4)\n                    if not len_bytes or len(len_bytes) != 4:\n                        break\n                except socket.timeout:\n                    continue\n                \n                msg_len = int.from_bytes(len_bytes, 'big')\n                \n                # Read message\n                data = b''\n                while len(data) < msg_len:\n                    chunk = client_socket.recv(min(4096, msg_len - len(data)))\n                    if not chunk:\n                        break\n                    data += chunk\n                \n                if len(data) != msg_len:\n                    break\n                \n                message = json.loads(data.decode())\n                response = self._process_message(message)\n                \n                # Send response\n                resp_data = json.dumps(response).encode()\n                client_socket.sendall(len(resp_data).to_bytes(4, 'big') + resp_data)\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[DIST-TX] Client handler error: {e}\")\n        finally:\n            try:\n                client_socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n    \n    def _process_message(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Process incoming message.\"\"\"\n        msg_type = message.get('type')\n        tx_id = message.get('tx_id')\n        \n        if msg_type == 'PREPARE_ACK':\n            return self._handle_prepare_ack(tx_id, message.get('node_id'), \n                                           message.get('success'))\n        \n        elif msg_type == 'COMMIT_ACK':\n            return self._handle_commit_ack(tx_id, message.get('node_id'))\n        \n        elif msg_type == 'ABORT_ACK':\n            return self._handle_abort_ack(tx_id, message.get('node_id'))\n        \n        elif msg_type == 'GET_STATUS':\n            return self._get_status(tx_id)\n        \n        return {'status': 'ERROR', 'message': 'Unknown message type'}\n    \n    def _handle_prepare_ack(self, tx_id: str, node_id: str, success: bool) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle prepare acknowledgement from participant.\"\"\"\n        tx = self.transactions.get(tx_id)\n        if not tx:\n            return {'status': 'ERROR', 'message': 'Transaction not found'}\n        \n        if success:\n            tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.PREPARED)\n        else:\n            tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.ABORTED)\n        \n        return {'status': 'OK'}\n    \n    def _handle_commit_ack(self, tx_id: str, node_id: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle     tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.COMMITTED)\n        return {'status': 'OK'}\n    \n    def _handle_abort_ack(self, tx_id: str, node_id: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle abort tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.ABORTED)\n        return {'status': 'OK'}\n    \n    def _get_status(self, tx_id: str) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Get transaction status.\"\"\"\n        tx = self.transactions.get(tx_id)\n        if not tx:\n            return {'status': 'ERROR', 'message': 'Transaction not found'}\n        \n        return {\n            'status': 'OK',\n ID.\n        \"\"\"\n        tx_id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        participants = list(self.participants.keys())\n        \n        tx = DistributedTransaction(tx_id, self.node_id, participants)\n  \n        print(f\"[DIST-TX] Started transaction {tx_id} with {len(participants)} participants\")\n        return tx_id\n    \n    def prepare_phase(self, tx_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n      \n        tx.update_state(TransactionState.PREPARING)\n        self._log_transaction(tx, 'PREPARING')\n        \n        # Send PREPARE to all participants\n        prepare_msg = {\n            'type': 'PREPARE',\n            'tx_id': tx_id,\n            'coordinator': self.node_id,\n            'operations': tx.operations\n        }\n        \n        threads = []\n        for node_id, conn       )\n            threads.append(t)\n            t.start()\n        \n        # Wait for all responses with timeout\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join(timeout=30)\n        \n        # Check results\n        if tx.any_aborted() or tx.any_failed():\n            tx.update_state(TransactionState.ABORTING)\n            self._log_transaction(tx, 'ABORTING')\n            return False\n        \n        if tx.all_prepared():\n            tx.update_state(TransactionState.PREPARED)\n            self._log_transaction(tx, 'PREPARED')\n            return True\n        \n        # Timeout or incomplete\n        tx.update_state(TransactionState.ABORTING)\n        self._log_transaction(tx, 'ABORTING_TIMEOUT')\n        return False\n    \n    def _send_prepare(self, tx: DistributedTransaction, node_id: str, \n                     conn: ParticipantConnection, message: Dict):\n        \"\"\"Send prepare message to a participant.\"\"\"\n        response = conn.send_receive(message, timeout=30)\n        \n        if response and response.get('status') == 'PREPARED':\n            tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.PREPARED)\n        elif response and response.get('status') == 'NO':\n            tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.ABORTED)\n        else:\n            tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.FAILED)\n    \n    def commit_phase(self, tx_id: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"\n        Phase 2: Commit the transaction.\n        Returns True if commit successful.\n        \"\"\"\n        tx = self.transactions.get(tx_id)\n        if not tx:\n            return False\n        \n        tx.update_state(TransactionState.COMMITTING)\n        self._log_transaction(tx, 'COMMITTING')\n        \n threads = []\n        for node_id, conn in self.participants.items():\n            t = threading.Thread(\n                target=self._send_commit,\n                args=(tx, node_id, conn, commit_msg),\n                daemon=True\n            )\n            threads.append(t)\n            t.start()\n        \n        # Wait for acknowledgements\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join(timeout=30)\n        \n        tx.update_state(TransactionState.COMMITTED)\n        self._log_transaction(tx, 'COMMITTED')\n        \n        print(f\"[DIST-TX] Transaction {tx_id} committed\")\n        return True\n    \n    def _send_commit(self, tx: DistributedTransaction, node_id: str,\n                    conn: ParticipantConnection, message: Dict):\n        \"\"\"Send commit message to a participant.\"\"\"\n        # Retry up to 3 times\n        for attempt in range(3):\n            response = conn.send_receive(message, timeout=30)\n            if response and response.get('status') == 'ACK':\n                tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.COMMITTED)\n                return\n            time.sleep(0.5 * (2 ** attempt))  # Exponential backoff\n        \n        # Mark as failed but don't stop - participant will check status\n        tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.FAILED)\n    \n    def abort_transaction(self, tx_id: str):\n        \"\"\"Abort a transaction.\"\"\"\n        tx = self.transactions.get(tx_id)\n        if not tx:\n            return\n        \n \"\"\"Send abort message to a participant.\"\"\"\n        conn.send_receive(message, timeout=10)\n        tx.update_participant(node_id, ParticipantState.ABORTED)\n    \n    def self.committed_transactions:\n                        return {'status': 'ACK'}  # Already committed\n                    return {'status': 'ERROR', 'message': 'Transaction not prepared'}\n    'schema': schema,\n                    'rows': table_data\n                }\n                total_rows += len(table_data)\n            \n            # Add metadata\n            backup_data['table_count'] = len([t for t in tables if not t.startswith('_')])\n            backup_data['row_count'] = total_rows\n            \n            # Add integrity checksum\n            data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n            hash_bytes = json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()\n            backup_data['checksum'] = hashlib.sha256(hash_bytes).hexdigest()\n            \n            # Write compressed JSON\n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'wt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                json.dump(backup_data, f, indent=2)\n            \n            # Restore original database if different\n            if client_state.get('current_db') and client_state['current_db'] != db_name:\n                self.db.use_database(client_state['current_db'])\n            \n            size_mb = os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024 * 1024)\n            return f\"OK: Backup complete - Backup failed - {e}\"\n\n\nclass RestoreDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    \"\"\"RESTORE DATABASE <name> FROM <file> - Import from JSON backup with integrity check.\"\"\"\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database', 'file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name and file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('is_admin'):\n            return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        \n        import json\n        import gzip\n        import os\n        import hashlib\n        \n        db_name = params['database']\n        file_path = params['file']\n        \n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        if not os.path.exists(file_path):\n            return f\"ERROR: Backup file not found: {file_path}\"\n        \n        # Verify integrity before restore\n        try:\n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'rt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                backup_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            if 'checksum' in backup_data:\n                stored_checksum = backup_data['checksum']\n                data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n                expected = hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()).hexdigest()\n                if stored_checksum != expected:\n                    return \"ERROR: Integrity check failed - checksum mismatch, file may be corrupted\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Cannot read backup file: {e}\"\n        \n        try:\n            if 'version' not in backup_data or 'tables' not in backup_data:\n                return \"ERROR: Invalid backup file format\"\n            \n            # Show source info\n            source_db = backup_data.get('database', 'unknown')\n            source_time = backup_data.get('created_at', 'unknown')\n            \n            self.db.create_database(db_name)\n            self.db.use_database(db_name)\n            \n            tables_restored = 0\n            rows_restored = 0\n            \n            for table_name, table_info in backup_data['tables'].items():\n                schema = table_info.get('schema', {})\n                rows = table_info.get('rows', [])\n                \n                columns = schema.get('columns', [])\n                if columns:\n                    self.db.create_table(table_name, columns)\n                \n                for row in rows:\n                    values = [row.get(col) for col in columns]\n                    self.db.insert(table_name, values)\n                    rows_restored += 1\n                \n                tables_restored += 1\n            \n            return f\"OK: Restored {tables_restored} tables, {rows_restored} rows from {source_db} ({source_time})\"\n            \n        except json.JSONDecodeError:\n            return \"ERROR: Invalid JSON in backup file\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Restore failed - {e}\"\n\n\nclass BackupTableCommand(Command):\n    \"\"\"BACKUP TABLE <name> TO <file> - Export single table to JSON with integrity check.\"\"\"\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table', 'file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name and file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        \n        import json\n        import gzip\n        import hashlib\n        from datetime import datetime\n        \n        table_name = params['table']\n        file_path = params['file']\n        \n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        try:\n            schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n            schema_data = self.db._db.get(schema_key)\n            if not schema_data:\n                return f\"ERROR: Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n            \n            schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n            \n            rows = []\n            prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n            for key, value in self.db._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                    continue\n                row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                rows.append(row)\n            \n            backup_data = {\n                'version': '1.0',\n                'database': client_state.get('current_db'),\n                'table': table_name,\n                'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                'schema': schema,\n                'rows': rows,\n Tuple, Callable\nfrom enum import Enum, auto\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom collections import deque\nimport select\n\n\nclass NodeState(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Raft node states.\"\"\"\n    FOLLOWER = \"follower\"\n    CANDIDATE = \"candidate\"\n    LEADER = \"leader\"\n\n\nclass LogEntry:\n    \"\"\"Single entry in the replicated log.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, term: int, index: int, command: Dict[str, Any]):\n        self.term = term\n        self.index = index\n        self.command = command\n        self.committed = False\n    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        return {\n            'term': self.term,\n            'index': self.index,\n            'command': self.command,\n            'committed': self.committed\n        }\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass NodeInfo:\n    \"\"\"Information about a cluster node.\"\"\"\n    node_id: str\n    host: str\n    port: int\n    last_heartbeat: float = field(default_factory=time.time)\n    is_alive: bool = True\n    match_index: int = 0\n    next_index: int = 1\n\n\nclass RaftConsensus:\n    \"\"\"\n    Raft consensus implementation for leader election and log replication.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, host: str, port: int, \n                 peers: List[Tuple[str, str, int]], \n                 on_leader_elected: Optional[Callable] = None,\n                 on_follower_promoted: Optional[Callable] = None):\n        self.node_id = node_id\n        self.host = host\n        self.port = port\n        self.peers: Dict[str, NodeInfo] = {}\n        \n        for peer_id, peer_host, peer_port in peers:\n            self.peers[peer_id] = NodeInfo(peer_id, peer_host, peer_port)\n        \n        self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n        self.current_term = 0\n        self.voted_for: Optional[str] = None\n        self.log: List[LogEntry] = []\n        self.commit_index = 0\n        self.last_applied = 0\n        \n        # Volatile state\n        self.leader_id: Optional[str] = None\n        self.election_timeout = random.uniform(0.15, 0.3)  # 150-300ms\n        self.heartbeat_interval = 0.05  # 50ms\n        self.last_heartbeat_time = time.time()\n        \n        # Callbacks\n        self.on_leader_elected = on_leader_elected\n        self.on_follower_promoted = on_follower_promoted\n        \n        # Networking\n        self.server_socket: Optional[socket.socket] = None\n        self.running = False\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        \n        # Vote counting\n        self.votes_received = 0\n        \n        # Apply queue\n        self._apply_queue: deque = deque()\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start the Raft node.\"\"\"\n        self.running = True\n        \n        # Start server\n        self.server_socket = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n        self.server_socket.setsockopt(socket.SOL_SOCKET, socket.SO_REUSEADDR, 1)\n        self.server_socket.bind((self.host, self.port))\n        self.server_socket.listen(10)\n        \n        print(f\"[RAFT] Node {self.node_id} started on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n        \n        # Start threads\n        threads = [\n            threading.Thread(target=self._accept_loop, daemon=True),\n            threading.Thread(target=self._election_timer, daemon=True),\n            threading.Thread(target=self._heartbeat_sender, daemon=True),\n            threading.Thread(target=self._log_applier, daemon=True)\n        ]\n        \n        for t in threads:\n            t.start()\n        \n        return threads\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop the Raft node.\"\"\"\n        self.running = False\n        if self.server_socket:\n            try:\n                self.server_socket.close()\n            except:\n                pass\n    \n    def _accept_loop(self):\n        \"\"\"Accept incoming connections.\"\"\"\n        while self.running:\n            try:\n                self.server_socket.settimeout(1.0)\n                client_socket, address = self.server_socket.accept()\n                handler = threading.Thread(\n                    target=self._handle_connection,\n                    args=(client_socket, address),\n                    daemon=True\n                )\n                handler.start()\n            except socket.timeout:\n                continue\n            except Exception as e:\n                if self.running:\n                    print(f\"[RAFT] Accept error: {e}\")\n    \n    def _handle_connection(self, client_socket: socket.socket, address: Tuple[str, int]):\n        \"\"\"Handle incoming Raft RPC.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            data = client_socket.recv(65536)\n            if not data:\n                return\n            \n            message = json.loads(data.decode())\n            response = self._process_rpc(message)\n            \n            if response:\n                client_socket.sendall(json.dumps(response).encode())\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f\"[RAFT] Connection handler error: {e}\")\n        finally:\n            client_socket.close()\n    \n    def _send_rpc(self, node: NodeInfo, message: Dict) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Send RPC to a node.\"\"\"\n        try:\n            sock = socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM)\n            sock.settimeout(0.5)\n            sock.connect((node.host, node.port))\n            sock.sendall(json.dumps(message).encode())\n            \n            sock.settimeout(1.0)\n            data = b''\n            while True:\n                chunk = sock.recv(4096)\n                if not chunk:\n                    break\n                data += chunk\n            \n            sock.close()\n            return json.loads(data.decode()) if data else None\n        except Exception as e:\n            node.is_alive = False\n            return None\n    \n    def _process_rpc(self, message: Dict) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Process incoming RPC.\"\"\"\n        rpc_type = message.get('type')\n        \n        if rpc_type == 'RequestVote':\n            return self._handle_request_vote(message)\n        elif rpc_type == 'AppendEntries':\n            return self._handle_append_entries(message)\n        elif rpc_type == 'Heartbeat':\n            return self._handle_heartbeat(message)\n        \n        return None\n    \n    def _handle_request_vote(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle RequestVote RPC.\"\"\"\n        term = message.get('term', 0)\n        candidate_id = message.get('candidate_id')\n        last_log_index = message.get('last_log_index', 0)\n        last_log_term = message.get('last_log_term', 0)\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            # Reply false if term < currentTerm\n            if term < self.current_term:\n                return {'term': self.current_term, 'vote_granted': False}\n            \n            # If term > currentTerm, update term and convert to follower\n            if term > self.current_term:\n                self.current_term = term\n                self.voted_for = None\n                self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n            \n            # Check if we can vote for this candidate\n            can_vote = (self.voted_for is None or self.voted_for == candidate_id)\n            log_is_current = (last_log_term > self._last_log_term() or \n                            (last_log_term == self._last_log_term() and \n                             last_log_index >= len(self.log)))\n            \n            if can_vote and log_is_current:\n                self.voted_for = candidate_id\n                self.last_heartbeat_time = time.time()  # Reset timeout\n                return {'term': self.current_term, 'vote_granted': True}\n            \n            return {'term': self.current_term, 'vote_granted': False}\n    \n    def _handle_append_entries(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle AppendEntries RPC.\"\"\"\n        term = message.get('term', 0)\n        leader_id = message.get('leader_id')\n        prev_log_index = message.get('prev_log_index', 0)\n        prev_log_term = message.get('prev_log_term', 0)\n        entries = message.get('entries', [])\n        leader_commit = message.get('leader_commit', 0)\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            # Reply false if term < currentTerm\n            if term < self.current_term:\n                return {'term': self.current_term, 'success': False}\n            \n            # Update term and convert to follower\n            if term > self.current_term:\n                self.current_term = term\n                self.voted_for = None\n            \n            self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n            self.leader_id = leader_id\n            self.last_heartbeat_time = time.time()\n            \n            # Reply false if log doesn't contain entry at prevLogIndex\n            if prev_log_index > 0:\n                if prev_log_index > len(self.log):\n                    return {'term': self.current_term, 'success': False}\n                if self.log[prev_log_index - 1].term != prev_log_term:\n                    return {'term': self.current_term, 'success': False}\n            \n            # Append new entries\n            for i, entry_data in enumerate(entries):\n                index = prev_log_index + i + 1\n                if index <= len(self.log):\n                    # Existing entry conflicts with new one\n                    if self.log[index - 1].term != entry_data['term']:\n                        # Delete existing entry and all that follow it\n                        self.log = self.log[:index - 1]\n                        self.log.append(LogEntry(\n                            entry_data['term'],\n                            entry_data['index'],\n                            entry_data['command']\n                        ))\n                else:\n                    self.log.append(LogEntry(\n                        entry_data['term'],\n                        entry_data['index'],\n                        entry_data['command']\n                    ))\n            \n            # Update commit index\n            if leader_commit > self.commit_index:\n                self.commit_index = min(leader_commit, len(self.log))\n            \n            return {'term': self.current_term, 'success': True}\n    \n    def _handle_heartbeat(self, message: Dict) -> Dict:\n        \"\"\"Handle heartbeat from leader.\"\"\"\n        term = message.get('term', 0)\n        leader_id = message.get('leader_id')\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            if term >= self.current_term:\n                self.current_term = term\n                self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n                self.leader_id = leader_id\n                self.last_heartbeat_time = time.time()\n                self.voted_for = None\n        \n        return {'term': self.current_term, 'success': True}\n    \n    def _election_timer(self):\n        \"\"\"Monitor election timeout.\"\"\"\n        while self.running:\n            time.sleep(0.01)  # 10ms check interval\n            \n            with self._lock:\n                if self.state == NodeState.LEADER:\n                    continue\n                \n                elapsed = time.time() - self.last_heartbeat_time\n                if elapsed > self.election_timeout:\n                    self._start_election()\n    \n    def _start_election(self):\n        \"\"\"Start a new election.\"\"\"\n        self.state = NodeState.CANDIDATE\n        self.current_term += 1\n        self.voted_for = self.node_id\n        self.votes_received = 1\n        self.last_heartbeat_time = time.time()\n        \n        print(f\"[RAFT] {self.node_id} starting election for term {self.current_term}\")\n        \n        # Request votes from all peers\n        message = {\n            'type': 'RequestVote',\n            'term': self.current_term,\n            'candidate_id': self.node_id,\n            'last_log_index': len(self.log),\n            'last_log_term': self._last_log_term()\n        }\n        \n        threads = []\n        for node in self.peers.values():\n            t = threading.Thread(\n                target=self._request_vote,\n                args=(node, message),\n                daemon=True\n            )\n            threads.append(t)\n            t.start()\n        \n        # Wait for votes with timeout\n        for t in threads:\n            t.join(timeout=0.3)\n        \n        # Check if we won\n        with self._lock:\n            if self.state == NodeState.CANDIDATE and self.votes_received > (len(self.peers) + 1) / 2:\n                self._become_leader()\n    \n    def _request_vote(self, node: NodeInfo, message: Dict):\n        \"\"\"Request vote from a peer.\"\"\"\n        response = self._send_rpc(node, message)\n        \n        if response:\n            with self._lock:\n                if response.get('term') > self.current_term:\n                    self.current_term = response['term']\n                    self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n                    self.voted_for = None\n                elif response.get('vote_granted'):\n                    self.votes_received += 1\n    \n    def _become_leader(self):\n        \"\"\"Convert to leader.\"\"\"\n        self.state = NodeState.LEADER\n        self.leader_id = self.node_id\n        \n        # Initialize leader state\n        for node in self.peers.values():\n            node.next_index = len(self.log) + 1\n            node.match_index = 0\n        \n        print(f\"[RAFT] {self.node_id} became leader for term {self.current_term}\")\n        \n        if self.on_leader_elected:\n            try:\n                self.on_leader_elected(self.node_id)\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[RAFT] Leader elected callback error: {e}\")\n    \n    def _heartbeat_sender(self):\n        \"\"\"Send heartbeats to followers.\"\"\"\n        while self.running:\n            time.sleep(self.heartbeat_interval)\n            \n            with self._lock:\n                if self.state != NodeState.LEADER:\n                    continue\n            \n            # Send heartbeats/AppendEntries to all peers\n            for node in self.peers.values():\n                threading.Thread(\n                    target=self._send_append_entries,\n                    args=(node,),\n                    daemon=True\n                ).start()\n    \n    def _send_append_entries(self, node: NodeInfo):\n        \"\"\"Send AppendEntries to a follower.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if self.state != NodeState.LEADER:\n                return\n            \n            prev_index = node.next_index - 1\n            prev_term = self.log[prev_index - 1].term if prev_index > 0 and prev_index <= len(self.log) else 0\n            \n            entries = []\n            for i in range(node.next_index - 1, len(self.log)):\n                entries.append(self.log[i].to_dict())\n            \n            message = {\n                'type': 'AppendEntries',\n                'term': self.current_term,\n                'leader_id': self.node_id,\n                'prev_log_index': prev_index,\n                'prev_log_term': prev_term,\n                'entries': entries,\n                'leader_commit': self.commit_index\n            }\n        \n        response = self._send_rpc(node, message)\n        \n        if response:\n            with self._lock:\n                if response.get('term') > self.current_term:\n                    self.current_term = response['term']\n                    self.state = NodeState.FOLLOWER\n                    self.voted_for = None\n                    return\n                \n                if response.get('success'):\n                    node.match_index = prev_index + len(entries)\n                    node.next_index = node.match_index + 1\n                else:\n                    node.next_index = max(1, node.next_index - 1)\n    \n    def _log_applier(self):\n        \"\"\"Apply committed entries to state machine.\"\"\"\n        while self.running:\n            time.sleep(0.01)\n            \n            with self._lock:\n                while self.last_applied < self.commit_index:\n                    self.last_applied += 1\n                    entry = self.log[self.last_applied - 1]\n                    entry.committed = True\n                    self._apply_queue.append(entry)\n    \n    def _last_log_term(self) -> int:\n        \"\"\"Get term of last log entry.\"\"\"\n        if not self.log:\n            return 0\n        return self.log[-1].term\n    \n    def propose(self, command: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Propose a command to the log.\n        Only works if this node is the leader.\n        \"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            if self.state != NodeState.LEADER:\n                if self.leader_id:\n                    return False, f\"Not leader. Current leader: {self.leader_id}\"\n                return False, \"No leader elected\"\n            \n            entry = LogEntry(\n                self.current_term,\n                len(self.log) + 1,\n                command\n            )\n            self.log.append(entry)\n            \n            # Replicate to majority\n            return self._replicate_entry(entry)\n    \n    def _replicate_entry(self, entry: LogEntry) -> Tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:\n        \"\"\"Replicate entry to majority of followers.\"\"\"\n        success_count = 1  # Count self\n        \n        threads = []\n        results = []\n        \n        def replicate_to(node: NodeInfo):\n            response = self._send_append_entries_sync(node, entry)\n            results.append(response is not None and response.get('success'))\n        \n        for node in self.peers.values():\n            t = threading.Thread(target=replicate_to, args=(node,), daemon=True)\n            threads.append(t)\n            t.start()\n        \n        for t in threads:\n            t.join(timeout=1.0)\n        \n        success_count += sum(1 for r in results if r)\n        \n        if success_count > (len(self.peers) + 1) / 2:\n            # Majority achieved, commit\n            with self._lock:\n                if entry.index > self.commit_index:\n                    self.commit_index = entry.index\n            return True, None\n        \n        return False, \"Failed to replicate to majority\"\n    \n    def _send_append_entries_sync(self, node: NodeInfo, entry: LogEntry) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Send single entry to follower synchronously.\"\"\"\n        message = {\n            'type': 'AppendEntries',\n            'term': self.current_term,\n            'leader_id': self.node_id,\n            'prev_log_index': entry.index - 1,\n            'prev_log_term': self.log[entry.index - 2].term if entry.index > 1 else 0,\n            'entries': [entry.to_dict()],\n            'leader_commit': self.commit_index\n        }\n        return self._send_rpc(node, message)\n    \n    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get current node status.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            return {\n                'node_id': self.node_id,\n                'state': self.state.value,\n                'term': self.current_term,\n                'leader': self.leader_id,\n                'log_size': len(self.log),\n                'commit_index': self.commit_index,\n                'last_applied': self.last_applied,\n                'peers': {\n                    node_id: {\n                        'alive': node.is_alive,\n                        'match_index': node.match_index\n                    }\n                    for node_id, node in self.peers.items()\n                }\n            }\n\n\nclass FailoverManager:\n    \"\"\"\n    Manages automatic failover using Raft consensus.\n    Coordinates with replication for seamless failover.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, node_id: str, host: str, port: int,\n                 peers: List[Tuple[str, str, int]],\n                 db=None, replication_client=None):\n        self.node_id = node_id\n        self.db = db\n        self.replication_client = replication_client\n        \n        self.raft = RaftConsensus(\n            node_id, host, port, peers,\n            on_leader_elected=self._on_leader_elected,\n            on_follower_promoted=self._on_follower_promoted\n        )\n        \n        self.is_primary = False\n        self.health_check_interval = 5.0\n        self._health_thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n        self.running = False\n    \n    def start(self):\n        \"\"\"Start failover manager.\"\"\"\n        self.running = True\n        self.raft.start()\n        \n        # Start health monitoring\n        self._health_thread = threading.Thread(target=self._health_monitor, daemon=True)\n        self._health_thread.start()\n        \n        print(f\"[FAILOVER] Manager started for node {self.node_id}\")\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop failover manager.\"\"\"\n        self.running = False\n        self.raft.stop()\n    \n    def _on_leader_elected(self, leader_id: str):\n        \"\"\"Called when this node becomes leader.\"\"\"\n        self.is_primary = True\n        print(f\"[FAILOVER] Node {self.node_id} became PRIMARY\")\n        \n        # Start accepting writes\n        if self.db:\n            # Promote to read-write mode\n            pass\n    \n    def _on_follower_promoted(self, leader_id: str):\n        \"\"\"Called when another node becomes leader.\"\"\"\n        self.is_primary = False\n        print(f\"[FAILOVER] <!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>monitoring.py</fileName>\n<contentOfFile>\"\"\"\nMonitoring and Metrics System for LevelDB Socket Server\n\nProvides performance metrics, health checks, and monitoring endpoints.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport time\nimport threading\nimport json\nimport statistics\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional, Callable\nfrom collections import deque\nfrom dataclasses import dataclass, field\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport psutil\nimport os\n\n\nclass MetricType(Enum):\n    \"\"\"Types of metrics.\"\"\"\n    COUNTER = \"counter\"\n    GAUGE = \"gauge\"\n    HISTOGRAM = \"histogram\"\n    TIMER = \"timer\"\n\n\n@dataclass\nclass Metric:\n    \"\"\"Single metric data point.\"\"\"\n    name: str\n    metric_type: MetricType\n    value: float\n    timestamp: float\n    labels: Dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)\n\n\nclass MetricsRegistry:\n    \"\"\"\n    Central registry for all metrics.\n    Thread-safe storage and retrieval of metrics.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, max_history: int = 10000):\n        self._metrics: Dict[str, List[Metric]] = {}\n        self._counters: Dict[str, float] = {}\n        self._gauges: Dict[str, float] = {}\n        self._histograms: Dict[str, List[float]] = {}\n        self._max_history = max_history\n        self._lock = threading.RLock()\n        \n        # Callbacks for metric events\n        self._callbacks: List[Callable[[Metric], None]] = []\n    \n    def register_callback(self, callback: Callable[[Metric], None]):\n        \"\"\"Register a callback for metric events.\"\"\"\n        self._callbacks.append(callback)\n    \n    def increment_counter(self, name: str, value: float = 1.0, \n                          labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Increment a counter metric.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n            self._counters[key] = self._counters.get(key, 0) + value\n            \n            metric = Metric(\n                name=name,\n                metric_type=MetricType.COUNTER,\n                value=self._counters[key],\n                timestamp=time.time(),\n                labels=labels or {}\n            )\n            self._store_metric(metric)\n    \n    def set_gauge(self, name: str, value: float, \n                  labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Set a gauge metric.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n            self._gauges[key] = value\n            \n            metric = Metric(\n                name=name,\n                metric_type=MetricType.GAUGE,\n                value=value,\n                timestamp=time.time(),\n                labels=labels or {}\n            )\n            self._store_metric(metric)\n    \n    def record_histogram(self, name: str, value: float,\n                       labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Record a value in a histogram.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n            if key not in self._histograms:\n                self._histograms[key] = []\n            self._histograms[key].append(value)\n            \n            # Keep only last 1000 values\n            if len(self._histograms[key]) > 1000:\n                self._histograms[key] = self._histograms[key][-1000:]\n            \n            metric = Metric(\n                name=name,\n                metric_type=MetricType.HISTOGRAM,\n                value=value,\n                timestamp=time.time(),\n                labels=labels or {}\n            )\n            self._store_metric(metric)\n    \n    def record_timer(self, name: str, duration: float,\n                     labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None):\n        \"\"\"Record a timer duration.\"\"\"\n        self.record_histogram(name, duration, labels)\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            metric = Metric(\n                name=name,\n                metric_type=MetricType.TIMER,\n                value=duration,\n                timestamp=time.time(),\n                labels=labels or {}\n            )\n            self._store_metric(metric)\n    \n    def _make_key(self, name: str, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create storage key from name and labels.\"\"\"\n        if not labels:\n            return name\n        label_str = \",\".join(f\"{k}={v}\" for k, v in sorted(labels.items()))\n        return f\"{name}{{{label_str}}}\"\n    \n    def _store_metric(self, metric: Metric):\n        \"\"\"Store metric in history.\"\"\"\n        key = self._make_key(metric.name, metric.labels)\n        if key not in self._metrics:\n            self._metrics[key] = deque(maxlen=self._max_history)\n        self._metrics[key].append(metric)\n        \n        # Notify callbacks\n        for callback in self._callbacks:\n            try:\n                callback(metric)\n            except Exception:\n                pass\n    \n    def get_counter(self, name: str, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Get current counter value.\"\"\"\n        key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n        return self._counters.get(key, 0)\n    \n    def get_gauge(self, name: str, labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None) -> float:\n        \"\"\"Get current gauge value.\"\"\"\n        key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n        return self._gauges.get(key, 0)\n    \n    def get_histogram_stats(self, name: str, \n                           labels: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None) -> Dict[str, float]:\n        \"\"\"Get histogram statistics.\"\"\"\n        key = self._make_key(name, labels)\n        values = self._histograms.get(key, [])\n        \n        if not values:\n            return {'count': 0, 'sum': 0, 'min': 0, 'max': 0, 'avg': 0, 'p95': 0, 'p99': 0}\n        \n        sorted_values = sorted(values)\n        count = len(sorted_values)\n        \n        return {\n            'count': count,\n            'sum': sum(sorted_values),\n            'min': sorted_values[0],\n            'max': sorted_values[-1],\n            'avg': statistics.mean(sorted_values),\n            'p95': sorted_values[int(count * 0.95)] if count > 1 else sorted_values[0],\n            'p99': sorted_values[int(count * 0.99)] if count > 1 else sorted_values[0]\n        }\n    \n    def get_all_metrics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get all current metrics.\"\"\"\n        with self._lock:\n            result = {\n                'counters': dict(self._counters),\n                'gauges': dict(self._gauges),\n                'histograms': {}\n            }\n            \n            for key in self._histograms:\n                name_labels = self._parse_key(key)\n                result['histograms'][key] = self.get_histogram_stats(\n                    name_labels['name'], \n                    name_labels.get('labels')\n                )\n            \n            return result\n    \n    def _parse_key(self, key: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse key into name and labels.\"\"\"\n        if '{' not in key:\n            return {'name': key, 'labels': {}}\n        \n        name, labels_str = key.split('{', 1)\n        labels_str = labels_str.rstrip('}')\n        \n        labels = {}\n        for part in labels_str.split(','):\n            if '=' in part:\n                k, v = part.split('=', 1)\n                labels[k] = v\n        \n        return {'name': name, 'labels': labels}\n    \n    def export_prometheus(self) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Export metrics in Prometheus format.\"\"\"\n        lines = []\n        \n        with self._lock:\n            # Counters\n            for key, value in self._counters.items():\n                name_labels = self._parse_key(key)\n                name = name_labels['name'].replace('.', '_')\n                labels = name_labels.get('labels', {})\n                label_str = self._format_labels(labels)\n                lines.append(f\"# TYPE {name} counter\")\n                lines.append(f\"{name}{label_str} {value}\")\n            \n            # Gauges\n            for key, value in self._gauges.items():\n                name_labels = self._parse_key(key)\n                name = name_labels['name'].replace('.', '_')\n                labels = name_labels.get('labels', {})\n                label_str = self._format_labels(labels)\n                lines.append(f\"# TYPE {name} gauge\")\n                lines.append(f\"{name}{label_str} {value}\")\n            \n            # Histograms\n            for key, values in self._histograms.items():\n                if not values:\n                    continue\n                name_labels = self._parse_key(key)\n                name = name_labels['name'].replace('.', '_')\n                labels = name_labels.get('labels', {})\n                \n                stats = self.get_histogram_stats(name_labels['name'], \n                                                  name_labels.get('labels'))\n                \n                lines.append(f\"# TYPE {name} histogram\")\n                lines.append(f\"{name}_count{self._format_labels(labels)} {stats['count']}\")\n                lines.append(f\"{name}_sum{self._format_labels(labels)} {stats['sum']}\")\n                lines.append(f\"{name}_bucket{{le=\\\"+Inf\\\"}}{self._format_labels(labels)} {stats['count']}\")\n        \n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n    \n    def _format_labels(self, labels: Dict[str, str]) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format labels for Prometheus.\"\"\"\n        if not labels:\n            return \"\"\n        label_pairs = [f'{k}=\"{v}\"' for k, v in sorted(labels.items())]\n        return \"{\" + \",\".join(label_pairs) + \"}\"\n\n\nclass SystemMetricsCollector:\n    \"\"\"\n    Collects system-level metrics.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, registry: MetricsRegistry):\n        self.registry = registry\n        self.process = psutil.Process(os.getpid())\n        self._running = False\n        self._thread: Optional[threading.Thread] = None\n    \n    def start(self, interval: float = 10.0):\n        \"\"\"Start collecting system metrics.\"\"\"\n        self._running = True\n        self._thread = threading.Thread(target=self._collect_loop, \n                                          args=(interval,), daemon=True)\n        self._thread.start()\n    \n    def stop(self):\n        \"\"\"Stop collecting system metrics.\"\"\"\n        self._running = False\n    \n    def _collect_loop(self, interval: float):\n        \"\"\"Collect metrics in a loop.\"\"\"\n        while self._running:\n            try:\n                self._collect_once()\n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f\"[METRICS] Collection error: {e}\")\n            \n            time.sleep(interval)\n    \n    def _collect_once(self):\n        \"\"\"Collect metrics once.\"\"\"\n        # CPU\n        cpu_percent = self.process.cpu_percent()\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.cpu_percent', cpu_percent)\n        \n        # Memory\n        memory_info = self.process.memory_info()\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.memory_rss_bytes', memory_info.rss)\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.memory_vms_bytes', memory_info.vms)\n        \n        # Disk\n        disk_io = self.process.io_counters()\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.disk_read_bytes', disk_io.read_bytes)\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.disk_write_bytes', disk_io.write_bytes)\n        \n        # Network\n        net_io = psutil.net_io_counters()\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.net_sent_bytes', net_io.bytes_sent)\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.net_recv_bytes', net_io.bytes_recv)\n        \n        # Open files\n        open_files = len(self.process.open_files())\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.open_files', open_files)\n        \n        # Thread count\n        self.registry.set_gauge('system.threads', self.process.num_threads())\n        \n        # Load average (Unix only)\n        try:\n            load1, load5, load15 = os.getloadavg()\n            self.registry.set_gauge('system.load1', load1)\n            self.registry.set_gauge('system.load5', load5)\n            self.registry.set_gauge('system.load15', load15)\n        except AttributeError:\n            pass  # Windows doesn't have getloadavg\n\n\nclass QueryMetricsCollector:\n    \"\"\"\n    Collects database query metrics.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, registry: MetricsRegistry):\n        self.registry = registry\n    \n    def record_query(self, query_type: str, duration: float, \n                     success: bool = True, rows_affected: int = 0):\n        \"\"\"Record a query execution.\"\"\"\n        labels = {'type': query_type, 'status': 'success' if success else 'error'}\n        \n        # Counter for total queries\n        self.registry.increment_counter('queries.total', 1, labels)\n        \n        # Counter for errors\n        if not success:\n            self.registry.increment_counter('queries.errors', 1, {'type': query_type})\n        \n        # Timer for duration\n        self.registry.record_timer('queries.duration_seconds', duration, labels)\n        \n        # Gauge for rows affected (for INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE)\n        if rows_affected > 0:\n            self.registry.set_gauge('queries.rows_affected', rows_affected, \n                                     {'type': query_type})\n    \n    def record_connection(self, event: str):\n        \"\"\"Record connection event.\"\"\"\n        self.registry.increment_counter('connections.total', 1, {'event': event})\n\n\nclass HealthChecker:\n    \"\"\"\n    Health check system for the database server.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, db=None):\n        self.db = db\n        self.checks: Dict[str, Callable[[], Tuple[bool, str]]] = {}\n        self._last_results: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}\n    \n    def add_check(self, name: str, check_func: Callable[[], Tuple[bool, str]]):\n        \"\"\"Add a health check.\"\"\"\n        self.checks[name] = check_func\n    \n    def run_check(self, name: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Run a single health check.\"\"\"\n        if name not in self.checks:\n            return {'name': name, 'status': 'unknown', 'message': 'Check not found'}\n        \n        try:\n            healthy, message = self.checks[name]()\n            result = {\n                'name': name,\n                'status': 'healthy' if healthy else 'unhealthy',\n                'message': message,\n                'timestamp': time.time()\n            }\n        except Exception as e:\n            result = {\n                'name': name,\n                'status': 'error',\n                'message': str(e),\n                'timestamp': time.time()\n            }\n        \n        self._last_results[name] = result\n        return result\n       result = self.run_check(name)\n            results[name] = result\n            if result['status'] != 'healthy':\n                overall_healthy = False\n        \n        return {\n            'status': 'healthy' if overall_healthy else 'unhealthy',\n            'checks': results,\n            'timestamp': time.time()\n        }\n    \n    def get_last_result(self, name: str) -> metrics.\n    Supports Prometheus format and JSON.\n    \"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self, registry: MetricsRegistry, host: str = \"0.0.0.0\", \n                 port: int = 9090, health_checker:        registry = self.registry\n            health_checker = self.health_checker\n            \n            class MetricsHandler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):\n                def do_GET(self):\n                    if self.path == '/metrics':\n                        self.send_response(200)\n                        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'text/plain')\n                        self.end_headers()\n                        self.wfile.write(registry.export_prometheus().encode())\n                    \n                    elif self.path == '/health':\n                        self.send_response(200)\n                        self.send_header('Content-Type', 'application/json')\n                        self.end_headers()\n                        if health_checker:\n self.wfile.write(b'Not found')\n                \n                def log_message(self, format, *args):\n                    pass  # Suppress logs\n            \n            self.server = HTTPServer((self.host, self.port), MetricsHandler)\n            self._running = True\n            \n            print(f\"[METRICS] HTTP exporter started on {self.host}:{self.port}\")\n            \n <!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "\"\"\"\nCommand Execution Framework for LevelDB Socket Server\n\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List\nfrom database import Database\n\n\nclass         return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        \n        try:\n            if self.db._system_db:\n                self.db._system_db.delete(b\"_replication:last_position\")\n                return BackupDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database', 'file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name and file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('is_admin'):\n            return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        \n        import json\n        import gzip\n        import os\n        import hashlib\n        from datetime import datetime\n        \n        db_name = params['database']\n        file_path = params['file']\n        \n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        try:\n            result = self.db.use_database(db_name)\n            if result.startswith(\"Database\"):\n                return f\"ERROR: {result}\"\n            \n            backup_data = {\n                'version': '1.0',\n                'database': db_name,\n                'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                'tables': {}\n            }\n            \n            tables = self.db.list_tables()\n            total_rows = 0\n            \n            for table_name in tables:\n                if table_name.startswith('_'):\n                    continue\n                \n                table_data = []\n                prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n                for key, value in self.db._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                    if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                        continue\n                    row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                    table_data.append(row)\n                \n                schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n                schema_data = self.db._db.get(schema_key)\n                schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode()) if schema_data else {}\n                \n                backup_data['tables'][table_name] = {\n                    'schema': schema,\n                    'rows': table_data\n                }\n                total_rows += len(table_data)\n            \n            backup_data['table_count'] = len([t for t in tables if not t.startswith('_')])\n            backup_data['row_count'] = total_rows\n            \n            data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n            hash_bytes = json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()\n            backup_data['checksum'] = hashlib.sha256(hash_bytes).hexdigest()\n            \n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'wt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                json.dump(backup_data, f, indent=2)\n            \n            if client_state.get('current_db') and client_state['current_db'] != db_name:\n                self.db.use_database(client_state['current_db'])\n            \n            size_mb = os.path.getsize(file_path) / (1024 * 1024)\n            return f\"OK: Backup complete - {backup_data['table_count']} tables, {total_rows} rows, {size_mb:.2f} MB\"\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Backup failed - {e}\"\n\n\nclass RestoreDatabaseCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['database', 'file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Database name and file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('is_admin'):\n            return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        \n        import json\n        import gzip\n        import os\n        import hashlib\n        \n        db_name = params['database']\n        file_path = params['file']\n        \n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        if not os.path.exists(file_path):\n            return f\"ERROR: Backup file not found: {file_path}\"\n        \n        try:\n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'rt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                backup_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            if 'checksum' in backup_data:\n                stored_checksum = backup_data['checksum']\n                data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n                expected = hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()).hexdigest()\n                if stored_checksum != expected:\n                    return \"ERROR: Integrity check failed - checksum mismatch\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Cannot read backup file: {e}\"\n        \n        try:\n            if 'version' not in backup_data or 'tables' not in backup_data:\n                return \"ERROR: Invalid backup file format\"\n            \n            source_db = backup_data.get('database', 'unknown')\n            source_time = backup_data.get('created_at', 'unknown')\n            \n            self.db.create_database(db_name)\n            self.db.use_database(db_name)\n            \n            tables_restored = 0\n            rows_restored = 0\n            \n            for table_name, table_info in backup_data['tables'].items():\n                schema = table_info.get('schema', {})\n                rows = table_info.get('rows', [])\n                \n                columns = schema.get('columns', [])\n                if columns:\n                    self.db.create_table(table_name, columns)\n                \n                for row in rows:\n                    values = [row.get(col) for col in columns]\n                    self.db.insert(table_name, values)\n                    rows_restored += 1\n                \n                tables_restored += 1\n            \n            return f\"OK: Restored {tables_restored} tables, {rows_restored} rows from {source_db}\"\n            \n        except json.JSONDecodeError:\n            return \"ERROR: Invalid JSON in backup file\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Restore failed - {e}\"\n\n\nclass BackupTableCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['table', 'file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Table name and file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('current_db'):\n            return \"ERROR: No database selected\"\n        \n        import json\n        import gzip\n        import hashlib\n        from datetime import datetime\n        \n        table_name = params['table']\n        file_path = params['file']\n        \n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        try:\n            schema_key = f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()\n            schema_data = self.db._db.get(schema_key)\n            if not schema_data:\n                return f\"ERROR: Table '{table_name}' does not exist\"\n            \n            schema = json.loads(schema_data.decode())\n            \n            rows = []\n            prefix = f\"{table_name}:\".encode()\n            for key, value in self.db._db.iterator(prefix=prefix):\n                if key.startswith(f\"_schema:{table_name}\".encode()):\n                    continue\n                row = json.loads(value.decode())\n                rows.append(row)\n            \n            backup_data = {\n                'version': '1.0',\n                'database': client_state.get('current_db'),\n                'table': table_name,\n                'created_at': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n                'schema': schema,\n                'rows': rows,\n                'row_count': len(rows)\n            }\n            \n            data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n            backup_data['checksum'] = hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()).hexdigest()\n            \n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'wt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                json.dump(backup_data, f, indent=2)\n            \n            return f\"OK: Table '{table_name}' backed up - {len(rows)} rows\"\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Backup failed - {e}\"\n\n\nclass ListBackupsCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        import os\n        import glob\n        import gzip\n        import json\n        \n        path = params.get('path', '.')\n        if not os.path.isdir(path):\n            return f\"ERROR: Directory not found: {path}\"\n        \n        try:\n            backup_files = glob.glob(os.path.join(path, '*.json.gz'))\n            if not backup_files:\n                return \"OK: No backup files found\"\n            \n            lines = []\n            lines.append(\"-\" * 80)\n            lines.append(f\"{'Backup File':<35} {'Size':>10} {'Tables':>8} {'Rows':>10} {'Status':>8}\")\n            lines.append(\"-\" * 80)\n            \n            for backup_file in sorted(backup_files, reverse=True):\n                try:\n                    with gzip.open(backup_file, 'rt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                        data = json.load(f)\n                    \n                    filename = os.path.basename(backup_file)\n                    size = os.path.getsize(backup_file)\n                    \n                    if size < 1024:\n                        size_str = f\"{size} B\"\n                    elif size < 1024 * 1024:\n                        size_str = f\"{size/1024:.1f} KB\"\n                    else:\n                        size_str = f\"{size/(1024*1024):.1f} MB\"\n                    \n                    table_count = len(data.get('tables', {}))\n                    if table_count == 0 and 'table' in data:\n                        table_count = 1\n                    \n                    row_count = data.get('row_count', 0)\n                    if row_count == 0 and 'tables' in data:\n                        for t in data['tables'].values():\n                            row_count += len(t.get('rows', []))\n                    \n                    status = \"OK\" if 'checksum' in data else \"?\"\n                    lines.append(f\"{filename[:34]:<35} {size_str:>10} {table_count:>8} {row_count:>10} {status:>8}\")\n                except:\n                    filename = os.path.basename(backup_file)\n                    lines.append(f\"{filename[:34]:<35} {'?':>10} {'?':>8} {'?':>10} {'ERR':>8}\")\n            \n            lines.append(\"-\" * 80)\n            lines.append(f\"{len(backup_files)} backup(s) found\")\n            \n            return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: {e}\"\n\n\nclass VerifyBackupCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, params, client_state):\n        if not self.validate_params(params, ['file']):\n            return \"ERROR: Backup file path required\"\n        if not client_state.get('is_admin'):\n            return \"ERROR: Admin only\"\n        \n        import os\n        import gzip\n        import json\n        import hashlib\n        \n        file_path = params['file']\n        if not file_path.endswith('.json.gz'):\n            file_path += '.json.gz'\n        \n        if not os.path.exists(file_path):\n            return f\"ERROR: Backup file not found: {file_path}\"\n        \n        try:\n            with gzip.open(file_path, 'rt', encoding='utf-8') as f:\n                backup_data = json.load(f)\n            \n            if 'version' not in backup_data:\n                return \"ERROR: Missing 'version' field - invalid backup format\"\n            \n            has_checksum = 'checksum' in backup_data\n            \n            lines = []\n            lines.append(\"-\" * 50)\n            \n            if has_checksum:\n                stored_checksum = backup_data['checksum']\n                data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in backup_data.items() if k != 'checksum'}\n                expected = hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode()).hexdigest()\n                \n                if stored_checksum == expected:\n                    lines.append(\"Backup Verification: PASSED\")\n                else:\n                    lines.append(\"Backup Verification: FAILED\")\n                    lines.append(f\"Expected: {expected[:32]}...\")\n                    lines.append(f\"Found:    {stored_checksum[:32]}...\")\n                    return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n            else:\n                lines.append(\"Backup Verification: WARNING\")\n                lines.append(\"No checksum present - cannot verify integrity\")\n            \n            lines.append(\"-\" * 50)\n            lines.append(f\"File: {os.path.basename(file_path)}\")\n            lines.append(f\"Version: {backup_data.get('version', 'unknown')}\")\n            lines.append(f\"Database: {backup_data.get('database', 'unknown')}\")\n            lines.append(f\"Created: {backup_data.get('created_at', 'unknown')}\")\n            \n            if 'tables' in backup_data:\n                lines.append(f\"Tables: {len(backup_data['tables'])}\")\n                total_rows = sum(len(t.get('rows', [])) for t in backup_data['tables'].values())\n                lines.append(f\"Rows: {total_rows}\")\n            elif 'table' in backup_data:\n                lines.append(f\"Table: {backup_data['table']}\")\n                lines.append(f\"Rows: {len(backup_data.get('rows', []))}\")\n            \n            lines.append(\"-\" * 50)\n            return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n                \n        except gzip.BadGzipFile:\n            return \"ERROR: Invalid gzip file - may be corrupted\"\n        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Invalid JSON: {e}\"\n        except Exception as e:\n            return f\"ERROR: Verification failed: {e}\"\n\n\nclass BeginTransactionCommand(Command):\n    def execute(self, r'^\\s*USE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'CREATE_DB': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*CREATE\\s+DATABASE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s*$',\n         'SHOW_TABLES': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+TABLES\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_DATABASES': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+DATABASES\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_USERS': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+USERS\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_MASTER_STATUS': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*SHOW\\s+MASTER\\s+STATUS\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'SHOW_SLAVE_STATUS':
