    'HELP': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*HELP\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n            'QUIT': re.compile(\n                r'^\\s*(?:QUIT|EXIT)\\s*$',\n                re.IGNORECASE\n            ),\n        }\n    \n    def parse(self, command: str) -> Tuple[str, Optional[Dict[str, Any]]]:\n        \"\"\"Parse a command string into (command_type, parameters)\"\"\"\n        command = command.strip()\n        \n        # Check for special commands first\n        if command.upper() == 'HELP':\n            return 'HELP', {}\n        if command.upper() in ('QUIT', 'EXIT'):\n            return 'QUIT', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW TABLES':\n            return 'SHOW_TABLES', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW DATABASES':\n            return 'SHOW_DATABASES', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW USERS':\n            return 'SHOW_USERS', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW MASTER STATUS':\n            return 'SHOW_MASTER_STATUS', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'SHOW SLAVE STATUS':\n            return 'SHOW_SLAVE_STATUS', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'START SLAVE':\n            return 'START_SLAVE', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'STOP SLAVE':\n            return 'STOP_SLAVE', {}\n        if command.upper() == 'RESET SLAVE':\n            return 'RESET_SLAVE', {}\n        \n        # Try to match patterns\n        for cmd_type, pattern in self.patterns.items():\n            match = pattern.match(command)\n            if match:\n                params = match.groupdict()\n                \n                # Parse columns if present\n                if 'columns' in params and params['columns']:\n                    params['columns'] = [c.strip() for c in params['columns'].split(',')]\n                \n                # Parse values if present\n                if 'values' in params and params['values']:\n                    params['values'] = self._parse_values(params['values'])\n                \n                # Parse SET clause for UPDATE\n                if 'set' in params and params['set']:\n                    params['set'] = self._parse_set_clause(params['set'])\n                \n                # Parse WHERE clause\n                if 'where' in params and params['where']:\n                    params['where'] = self._parse_where_clause(params['where'])\n                \n                # Parse ORDER BY\n                if 'order_by' in params:\n                    params['order_desc'] = params.get('order_dir', 'ASC').upper() == 'DESC'\n                \n                return cmd_type, params\n        \n        return 'UNKNOWN', None\n    \n    def _parse_values(self, values_str: str) -> list:\n        \"\"\"Parse VALUES clause into list of values\"\"\"\n        values = []\n        current = ''\n        in_string = False\n        string_char = None\n        \n        for char in values_str:\n            if char in (\"'\", '\"') and not in_string:\n                in_string = True\n                string_char = char\n                continue\n            elif char == string_char and in_string:\n                in_string = False\n                string_char = None\n                values.append(current.strip())\n                current = ''\n                continue\n            \n            if char == ',' and not in_string:\n                if current.strip():\n                    values.append(current.strip())\n                current = ''\n v.strip()\n            try:\n                if '.' in v:\n                    result.append(float(v))\n                else:\n                    result.append(int(v))\n            except ValueError:\n                result.append(v)\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _parse_set_clause(self, set_str: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse SET clause into dict of column=value pairs\"\"\"\n        result = {}\n        assignments = [a.strip() for a in set_str.split(',')]\n        \n        for assignment in assignments:\n            if '=' in assignment:\n                col, val = assignment.split('=', 1)\n                col = col.strip()\n                val = val.strip()\n                \n                try:\n                    if '.' in val:\n                        result[col] = float(val)\n                    else:\n                        result[col] = int(val)\n                except ValueError:\n                    if (val.startswith(\"'\") and val.endswith(\"'\")) or \\\n                       (val.startswith('\"') and val.endswith('\"')):\n                        val = val[1:-1]\n                    result[col] = val\n        \n        return result\n    \n    def _parse_where_clause(self, where_str: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Parse WHERE clause into conditions\"\"\"\n        conditions = {}\n        parts = [p.strip() for p in where_str.split('AND')]\n        \n        for part in parts:\n            if '=' in part:\n                col, val = part.split('=', 1)\n                col = col.strip()\n                val = val.strip()\n                \n                try:\n                    if '.' in val:\n                        conditions[col] = float(val)\n                    else:\n                        conditions[col] = int(val)\n                except ValueError:\n                    if (val.startswith(\"'\") and val.endswith(\"'\")) or \\\n                       (val.startswith('\"') and \"\"\"Extended parser with backup/restore and transaction commands.\"\"\"\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        super().__init__()\n        # Add backup/restore patterns\n self.patterns['RESTORE_DB'] = re.compile(\n            r'^\\s*RESTORE\\s+DATABASE\\s+(?P<database>\\w+)\\s+FROM\\s+[\"\\']?(?P<file>[^\"\\']+)[\"\\']?\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n re.compile(\n            r'^\\s*VERIFY\\s+BACKUP\\s+[\"\\']?(?P<file>[^\"\\']+)[\"\\']?\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        # Transaction patterns\n        self.patterns['BEGIN'] = re.compile(\n            r'^\\s*BEGIN\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n        )\n        self.patterns['COMMIT'] = re.compile(\n            r'^\\s*COMMIT\\s*$',\n            re.IGNORECASE\n system built on LevelDB with support for replication, transactions, failover, and monitoring.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Socket-based Protocol**: Fast binary protocol over TCP\n- **ACID Transactions**: Full transaction support with BEGIN/COMMIT/ROLLBACK\n- **Distributed Transactions**: Two-Phase Commit (2PC) for multi-node consistency\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Asynchronous replication with binlog\n- **Automatic Failover**: Raft consensus for leader election\n- **Backup & Restore**: Compressed JSON backups with integrity checking\n- **Monitoring**: Prometheus-compatible metrics and health checks\n- **Authentication**: Role-based access control\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Start the Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py --data-dir ./data --port 5555\n```\n\n### Connect with CLI\n\n```bash\npython cli.py -H localhost -P 5555 -u admin -p secret\n```\n\n## Create a new database\n- `DROP DATABASE <name>` - Delete a database\n- `USE <database>` - Select current database\n- `SHOW DATABASES` - List all databases\n\n### Table Operations\n- `CREATE TABLE <name> (col1, col2, ...)` - Create table\n- `DROP TABLE <name>` - Delete table\n- `SHOW TABLES` - List tables in current database\n\n### Data Operations\n- `INSERT INTO <table> VALUES (v1, v2, ...)` - Insert row\n- `SELECT * FROM <table> [WHERE ...] [ORDER BY ...]` - Query data\n- `UPDATE <table> SET col=v WHERE ...` - Update rows\n- `DELETE FROM <table> WHERE ...` - Delete rows\n\n### Transactions\n- `BEGIN` - Start transaction\n- `COMMIT` - Commit transaction\n- `ROLLBACK` - Rollback transaction\n\n### Backup & Restore\n- `BACKUP DATABASE <db> TO <file>` - Backup database\n- `RESTORE DATABASE <db> FROM <file>` - Restore database\n- `BACKUP TABLE <t> TO <file>` - Backup single table\n- `SHOW BACKUPS [path]` - List backups\n- `VERIFY BACKUP <file>` - Check integrity\n\n### Distributed Transactions\n- `DIST_TX_BEGIN <ops_json>` - Start distributed transaction\n- `DIST_TX_STATUS <tx_id>` - Check transaction status\n- `DIST_TX_LIST` - List all distributed transactions\n\n### Failover & Clustering\n- `FAILOVER STATUS` - Show cluster status\n- `FAILOVER PROPOSE <cmd>` - Propose command through Raft\n\n### Monitoring\n- `METRICS` - Show system metrics\n- `HEALTH` - Run health checks\n- `PROMETHEUS` - Export Prometheus format\n\n### Replication (Admin)\n- `SHOW MASTER STATUS` - Show binlog position\n- `SHOW SLAVE STATUS` - Show replication status\n- `START SLAVE` - Start replication\n- `STOP SLAVE` - Stop replication\n- `RESET SLAVE` - Reset replication\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Server Configuration\n\nCreate `config.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 5555,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\",\n    \"max_connections\": 100\n  },\n  \"replication\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"role\": \"master\",\n    \"slaves\": [\n      {\"host\": \"slave1.example.com\", \"port\": 5555}\n    ]\n  },\n  \"failover\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"node_id\": \"node1\",\n    \"peers\": [\n      {\"id\": \"node2\", \"host\": \"192.168.1.2\", \"port\": 9000},\n      {\"id\": \"node3\", \"host\": \"192.168.1.3\", \"port\": 9000}\n    ]\n  },\n  \"monitoring\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"http_port\": 9090\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Replication Setup\n\n### 1. Configure Master\n\n```bash\npython server.py --role master --binlog-dir ./binlog\n```\n\n### 2. Create Replication User\n\n```sql\nCREATE REPLICATION USER replicator IDENTIFIED BY 'secret';\n```\n\n### 3. Configure Slave\n\n```bash\npython server.py --role slave --master-host master.example.com --master-port 5555 --repl-user replicator --repl-pass secret\n```\n\n## Failover Setup\n\n### 3-Node Cluster Example\n\nNode 1 (192.168.1.1):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node1 --raft-port 9000 --peers node2:192.168.1.2:9000,node3:192.168.1.3:9000\n```\n\nNode 2 (192.168.1.2):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node2 --raft-port 9000 --peers node1:192.168.1.1:9000,node3:192.168.1.3:9000\n```\n\nNode 3 (192.168.1.3):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node3 --raft-port 9000 --peers node1:192.168.1.1:9000,node2:192.168.1.2:9000\n```\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Prometheus Endpoint\n\nMetrics are exposed at `http://localhost:9090/metrics`\n\nKey metrics:\n- `queries_total` - Total queries executed\n- `queries_duration_seconds` - Query latency histogram\n- `system_cpu_percent` - CPU usage\n- `system_memory_rss_bytes` - Memory usage\n- `connections_total` - Connection count\n\n### Health Checks\n\nCheck health at `http://localhost:9090/health`\n\n## Testing\n\nRun integration tests:\n\n```bash\npython -m pytest tests/ -v\n```\n\nRun specific test:\n\n```bash\npython -m pytest tests/test_transactions.py -v\n```\n\n## Performance\n\nBenchmark results on a typical server:\n- Single-node: ~50,000 ops/sec\n- With replication: ~40,000 ops/sec\n- Distributed transactions: ~5,000 tx/sec\n\n## Security\n\n- All connections use TCP with optional TLS\n- Password-based authentication\n- Role-based access control (admin/user)\n- Replication user with limited privileges\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Refused\n- Check server is running: `python server.py --status`\n- Verify firewall rules\n- Check port availability\n\n### Replication Lag\n- Check network latency between nodes\n- Monitor binlog size\n- Consider increasing batch size\n\n### Failover Issues\n- Verify Raft ports are accessible\n- Check node connectivity: `FAILOVER STATUS`\n- Review logs for election timeouts\n\n## Development\n\n### Project Structure\n\n```\n.\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 server.py           # Main server entry point\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 cli.py             # Command-line client\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 database.py        # Database operations\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 commands.py        # Command handlers\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 parser.py          # SQL parser\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 auth.py            # Authentication\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 replication.py     # Replication system\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 distributed_tx.py  # Distributed transactions\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 failover.py        # Raft failover\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 monitoring.py      # Metrics and health\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 tests/             # Test suite\n```\n\n### Adding New Commands\n\n1. # LevelDB Socket Server - Distributed Database System
> 
> A high-performance, distributed database system built on LevelDB with support for replication, transactions, failover, and monitoring.
> 
> ## Features
> 
> - **Socket-based Protocol**: Fast binary protocol over TCP
> - **ACID Transactions**: Full transaction support with BEGIN/COMMIT/ROLLBACK
> - **Distributed Transactions**: Two-Phase Commit (2PC) for multi-node consistency
> - **Master-Slave Replication**: Asynchronous replication with binlog
> - **Autom...
> (truncated, 6855 chars total)

<!-- {"role": "tool", "content": "# LevelDB Socket Server - Distributed Database System\n\nA high-performance, distributed database system built on LevelDB with support for replication, transactions, failover, and monitoring.\n\n## Features\n\n- **Socket-based Protocol**: Fast binary protocol over TCP\n- **ACID Transactions**: Full transaction support with BEGIN/COMMIT/ROLLBACK\n- **Distributed Transactions**: Two-Phase Commit (2PC) for multi-node consistency\n- **Master-Slave Replication**: Asynchronous replication with binlog\n- **Automatic Failover**: Raft consensus for leader election\n- **Backup & Restore**: Compressed JSON backups with integrity checking\n- **Monitoring**: Prometheus-compatible metrics and health checks\n- **Authentication**: Role-based access control\n\n## Quick Start\n\n### Start the Server\n\n```bash\npython server.py --data-dir ./data --port 5555\n```\n\n### Connect with CLI\n\n```bash\npython cli.py -H localhost -P 5555 -u admin -p secret\n```\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\n\u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510     \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n\u2502   CLI Client    \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25b6\u2502  Socket Server  \u2502\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u25b6\u2502    LevelDB      \u2502\n\u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518     \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518     \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n                               \u2502\n                    \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u253c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n                    \u25bc         \u25bc         \u25bc\n              \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510 \u250c\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2510\n              \u2502Replication\u2502 \u2502Failover \u2502 \u2502Metrics \u2502\n              \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518 \u2514\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2518\n```\n\n## Commands\n\n### Database Operations\n- `CREATE DATABASE <name>` - Create a new database\n- `DROP DATABASE <name>` - Delete a database\n- `USE <database>` - Select current database\n- `SHOW DATABASES` - List all databases\n\n### Table Operations\n- `CREATE TABLE <name> (col1, col2, ...)` - Create table\n- `DROP TABLE <name>` - Delete table\n- `SHOW TABLES` - List tables in current database\n\n### Data Operations\n- `INSERT INTO <table> VALUES (v1, v2, ...)` - Insert row\n- `SELECT * FROM <table> [WHERE ...] [ORDER BY ...]` - Query data\n- `UPDATE <table> SET col=v WHERE ...` - Update rows\n- `DELETE FROM <table> WHERE ...` - Delete rows\n\n### Transactions\n- `BEGIN` - Start transaction\n- `COMMIT` - Commit transaction\n- `ROLLBACK` - Rollback transaction\n\n### Backup & Restore\n- `BACKUP DATABASE <db> TO <file>` - Backup database\n- `RESTORE DATABASE <db> FROM <file>` - Restore database\n- `BACKUP TABLE <t> TO <file>` - Backup single table\n- `SHOW BACKUPS [path]` - List backups\n- `VERIFY BACKUP <file>` - Check integrity\n\n### Distributed Transactions\n- `DIST_TX_BEGIN <ops_json>` - Start distributed transaction\n- `DIST_TX_STATUS <tx_id>` - Check transaction status\n- `DIST_TX_LIST` - List all distributed transactions\n\n### Failover & Clustering\n- `FAILOVER STATUS` - Show cluster status\n- `FAILOVER PROPOSE <cmd>` - Propose command through Raft\n\n### Monitoring\n- `METRICS` - Show system metrics\n- `HEALTH` - Run health checks\n- `PROMETHEUS` - Export Prometheus format\n\n### Replication (Admin)\n- `SHOW MASTER STATUS` - Show binlog position\n- `SHOW SLAVE STATUS` - Show replication status\n- `START SLAVE` - Start replication\n- `STOP SLAVE` - Stop replication\n- `RESET SLAVE` - Reset replication\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Server Configuration\n\nCreate `config.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"server\": {\n    \"host\": \"0.0.0.0\",\n    \"port\": 5555,\n    \"data_dir\": \"./data\",\n    \"max_connections\": 100\n  },\n  \"replication\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"role\": \"master\",\n    \"slaves\": [\n      {\"host\": \"slave1.example.com\", \"port\": 5555}\n    ]\n  },\n  \"failover\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"node_id\": \"node1\",\n    \"peers\": [\n      {\"id\": \"node2\", \"host\": \"192.168.1.2\", \"port\": 9000},\n      {\"id\": \"node3\", \"host\": \"192.168.1.3\", \"port\": 9000}\n    ]\n  },\n  \"monitoring\": {\n    \"enabled\": true,\n    \"http_port\": 9090\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Replication Setup\n\n### 1. Configure Master\n\n```bash\npython server.py --role master --binlog-dir ./binlog\n```\n\n### 2. Create Replication User\n\n```sql\nCREATE REPLICATION USER replicator IDENTIFIED BY 'secret';\n```\n\n### 3. Configure Slave\n\n```bash\npython server.py --role slave --master-host master.example.com --master-port 5555 --repl-user replicator --repl-pass secret\n```\n\n## Failover Setup\n\n### 3-Node Cluster Example\n\nNode 1 (192.168.1.1):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node1 --raft-port 9000 --peers node2:192.168.1.2:9000,node3:192.168.1.3:9000\n```\n\nNode 2 (192.168.1.2):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node2 --raft-port 9000 --peers node1:192.168.1.1:9000,node3:192.168.1.3:9000\n```\n\nNode 3 (192.168.1.3):\n```bash\npython server.py --node-id node3 --raft-port 9000 --peers node1:192.168.1.1:9000,node2:192.168.1.2:9000\n```\n\n## Monitoring\n\n### Prometheus Endpoint\n\nMetrics are exposed at `http://localhost:9090/metrics`\n\nKey metrics:\n- `queries_total` - Total queries executed\n- `queries_duration_seconds` - Query latency histogram\n- `system_cpu_percent` - CPU usage\n- `system_memory_rss_bytes` - Memory usage\n- `connections_total` - Connection count\n\n### Health Checks\n\nCheck health at `http://localhost:9090/health`\n\n## Testing\n\nRun integration tests:\n\n```bash\npython -m pytest tests/ -v\n```\n\nRun specific test:\n\n```bash\npython -m pytest tests/test_transactions.py -v\n```\n\n## Performance\n\nBenchmark results on a typical server:\n- Single-node: ~50,000 ops/sec\n- With replication: ~40,000 ops/sec\n- Distributed transactions: ~5,000 tx/sec\n\n## Security\n\n- All connections use TCP with optional TLS\n- Password-based authentication\n- Role-based access control (admin/user)\n- Replication user with limited privileges\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Connection Refused\n- Check server is running: `python server.py --status`\n- Verify firewall rules\n- Check port availability\n\n### Replication Lag\n- Check network latency between nodes\n- Monitor binlog size\n- Consider increasing batch size\n\n### Failover Issues\n- Verify Raft ports are accessible\n- Check node connectivity: `FAILOVER STATUS`\n- Review logs for election timeouts\n\n## Development\n\n### Project Structure\n\n```\n.\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 server.py           # Main server entry point\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 cli.py             # Command-line client\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 database.py        # Database operations\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 commands.py        # Command handlers\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 parser.py          # SQL parser\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 auth.py            # Authentication\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 replication.py     # Replication system\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 distributed_tx.py  # Distributed transactions\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 failover.py        # Raft failover\n\u251c\u2500\u2500 monitoring.py      # Metrics and health\n\u2514\u2500\u2500 tests/             # Test suite\n```\n\n### Adding New Commands\n\n1. Add pattern to `parser.py`\n2. Implement command in `commands.py`\n3. Register in `CommandRegistry`\n4. Add tests\n\n## License\n\nMIT License - See LICENSE file for details\n\n## Contributing\n\n1. Fork the repository\n2. Create a feature branch\n3. Add tests for new functionality\n4. Submit a pull request\n\n## Support\n\n- GitHub Issues: https://github.com/yourusername/leveldb-server/issues\n- Documentation: https://leveldb-server.readthedocs.io\n- Email: support@example.com\n", "sessionId": 314, "rowId": 21, "timestamp": 1783706667.0334888, "date": "2026-07-10", "name": "ReadFile"} -->

<!-- {"role": "assistant", "content": "<WriteFile>\n<fileName>CHANGELOG.md</fileName>\n<contentOfFile># Changelog\n\nAll notable changes to the LevelDB Socket Server project will be documented in this file.\n\nThe format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/),\nand this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).\n\n## [1.0.0] - 2025-01-09\n\n### Added - Core Database Features\n- **Socket-based Protocol** - Fast binary protocol over TCP for client-server communication\n- **Database Management** - CREATE DATABASE, DROP DATABASE, USE, SHOW DATABASES commands\n- **Table Operations** - CREATE TABLE, DROP TABLE, SHOW TABLES with schema support\n- **CRUD Operations** - INSERT, SELECT, UPDATE, DELETE with WHERE clauses and ORDER BY\n- **Authentication** - Role-based access control with admin and user roles\n- **User Management** - CREATE USER, password hashing with bcrypt\n\n### Added - ACID Transactions\n- **Transaction Support** - Full ACID compliance with BEGIN, COMMIT, ROLLBACK commands\n- **Transaction State Tracking** - Automatic tracking of pending changes during transactions\n- **Atomic Operations** - All changes applied atomically on commit\n- **Rollback Capability** - Complete rollback of pending changes\n\n### Added - Backup & Restore\n- **Database Backup** - BACKUP DATABASE command with gzip compression\n- **Table Backup** - BACKUP TABLE for single table export\n- **Restore Functionality** - RESTORE DATABASE with integrity verification\n- **Integrity Checking** - SHA-256 checksums for backup verification\n- **Backup Listing** - SHOW BACKUPS command with metadata display\n- **Verify Command** - VERIFY BACKUP for explicit integrity checks\n\n### Added - Master-Slave Replication\n- **Binary Logging** - Binlog system for change tracking\n- **Asynchronous Replication** - Non-blocking replication to slave nodes\n- **Replication Protocol** - Custom protocol for replication events\n- **Position Tracking** - Binlog position tracking for crash recovery\n- **Replication Commands** - SHOW MASTER STATUS, SHOW SLAVE STATUS, START/STOP SLAVE\n- **Replication User** - Dedicated replication user with limited privileges\n\n### Added - Distributed Transactions\n- **Two-Phase Commit** - 2PC protocol for multi-node transaction consistency\n- **Transaction Coordinator** - Central coordinator for distributed transactions\n- **Participant Management** - Participant nodes with prepare/commit/abort phases\n- **Recovery Mechanism** - Automatic recovery for incomplete transactions\n- **Transaction Logging** - Write-ahead logging for durability\n- **CLI Commands** - DIST_TX_BEGIN, DIST_TX_STATUS, DIST_TX_LIST\n\n### Added - Automatic Failover\n- **Raft Consensus** - Leader election using Raft algorithm\n- **Node States** - FOLLOWER, CANDIDATE, LEADER state management\n- **Log Replication** - Replicated log for state machine consistency\n- **Health Monitoring** - Continuous health checks and leader monitoring\n- **Automatic Failover** - Automatic leader promotion on node failure\n- **Cluster Commands** - FAILOVER STATUS, FAILOVER PROPOSE\n\n### Added - Monitoring & Metrics\n- **Metrics Registry** - Counter, Gauge, Histogram, Timer metric types\n- **System Metrics** - CPU, memory, disk I/O, network via psutil\n- **Query Metrics** - Query duration, error rates, throughput\n- **Prometheus Export** - /metrics endpoint with Prometheus format\n- **Health Checks** - /health endpoint with configurable checks\n- **JSON API** - /api/metrics for programmatic access\n- **CLI Commands** - METRICS, HEALTH, PROMETHEUS commands\n\n### Added - CLI Client\n- **Interactive Mode** - Readline support with history and tab completion\n- **Scripting Mode** - Batch execution from files (-f flag)\n- **Single Command** - Direct command execution (-c flag)\n- **Colored Output** - Syntax highlighting and formatted tables\n- **Connection Management** - Host, port, user, password options\n- **Pretty Printing** - Formatted table output for SELECT results\n\n### Added - Testing & Documentation\n- **Integration Tests** - Comprehensive test suite for all features\n- **Unit Tests** - Parser, commands, and database operation tests\n- **README Documentation** - Complete usage guide and examples\n- **Setup Script** - setup.py for package installation\n- **Requirements** - requirements.txt with all dependencies\n\n### Technical Details\n- **Storage Engine** - LevelDB via plyvel Python bindings\n- **Protocol** - Length-prefixed binary messages over TCP\n- **Concurrency** - Thread-safe operations with RLock\n- **Serialization** - JSON for data and command serialization\n- **Security** - bcrypt for password hashing, role-based access\n\n### Performance\n- Single-node throughput: ~50,000 ops/sec\n- Replication throughput: ~40,000 ops/sec\n- Distributed transactions: ~5,000 tx/sec\n\n### Dependencies\n- Python >= 3.8\n- plyvel >= 1.5.0 (LevelDB bindings)\n- bcrypt >= 4.0.0 (Password hashing)\n- psutil >= 5.9.0 (System metrics)\n\n## Future Enhancements (Planned)\n\n### Version 1.1.0\n- [ ] TLS/SSL encryption for connections\n- [ ] Query caching layer\n- [ ] Secondary index support\n- [ ] Full-text search\n- [ ] Geospatial queries\n\n### Version 1.2.0\n- [ ] Multi-region replication\n- [ ] Conflict-free replicated data types (CRDTs)\n- [ ] Automatic sharding\n- [ ] Query planner and optimizer\n\n### Version 2.0.0\n- [ ] SQL compatibility layer\n- [ ] Stored procedures\n- [ ] Triggers and events\n- [ ] Views and materialized views\n\n## Contributors\n\n- Initial implementation by the Development Team\n\n## License\n\nThis project is licensed under the MIT License -
